CONCEPT 4: "THE ALGORITHM KNOWS"

Genre Blend: Black Mirror "Hang the DJ" \+ Dating Reality Show Murder

📍 Setting/Location: Cancún, Mexico, 2025\. "Forever Match" reality show filming location—luxury resort. Contestants use AI dating algorithm that "guarantees" soulmate matches based on biometric/psychological data. Cameras everywhere.

👤 Victim: Terrence Baptiste, 33, Haitian-American contestant and tech investor. Caught cheating the algorithm—secretly dating multiple "non-match" contestants. Found dead in infinity pool, electrocuted.

🎭 Tone: Reality TV satire meets tech thriller. Love Island meets Black Mirror's dating dystopia. Performative romance, algorithm worship, contestants willing to kill for their "perfect match."

🔞 Adult Elements:

Explicit sexual content (reality show hot tub scenes)

Alcohol abuse (open bar, drunk contestants)

Steroid use (contestants enhancing appearances)

Emotional manipulation for ratings

Graphic electrocution description

Drug use (cocaine at afterparties)

Toxic masculinity and relationship violence

Privacy violations (24/7 surveillance)

🕵 Suspects (6) \- 100% POC:

Priya Desai (29, Indian-American) \- Contestant, Terrence's "algorithm match" but he rejected her on camera—humiliating

Jamal Rivers (31, Black American) \- Contestant, Terrence was secretly sleeping with his match

Mei Lin (27, Chinese-American) \- Producer, Terrence threatened to expose show's fake algorithm (scripted matches)

Carlos Vega (35, Mexican) \- Contestant, Terrence outed him as gay (Carlos was closeted for family reasons)

Aaliyah Khan (30, Pakistani-American) \- Contestant, Terrence spread rumors she had STDs, ruining her match chances

Diego Moreno (42, Dominican) \- Show host, Terrence blackmailing him over fake identity (previous fraud charges)

📅 Time Period: July 2025 (Week 3 of filming)

🧩 Complexity Elements \- EASY DIFFICULTY:

Murder during 2-hour window when cameras "malfunctioned" (suspicious timing)

Electrocution caused by hair dryer dropped in pool

Only 6 people had access to electrical equipment area

Simple clue: killer's fingerprints on hair dryer cord

Motive clear: Terrence ruined each suspect's chance at "algorithm love" or exposed damaging secrets

Red herring: another contestant threatened Terrence on camera but has solid alibi

🎯 Mystery Hook: In a reality show where an AI algorithm controls who you love, one contestant breaks the rules—and ends up dead. Terrence exposed the show's biggest secret: the "perfect algorithm" is fake. Someone killed him to protect either their shot at love, their reputation, or the show's $50M franchise. Easy solve: only 6 had access \+ fingerprints \+ clear motives.

# **🔍 COMPREHENSIVE HUB ANALYSIS: WHAT HAS BEEN BUILT**

## **📁 The Murder Mystery Project Ecosystem So Far**

Your hub represents a **substantial body of work** across multiple mystery games. Here's the full inventory:

---

### **🎭 MYSTERY 2A — "The Final Prescription"**

*Medical thriller, contemporary setting, Riverside Medical Institute*

A complete game was built including a full Story Bible HTML file, all AI chat prompts (35+), all image prompts (28+), and a complete set of HTML investigation documents saved to AI Drive — including police reports, crime scene reports, autopsy/toxicology/DNA reports, character dossiers, interview transcripts, and evidence photographs. Multiple image generation sessions produced character portraits, crime scene photos, evidence forensics, and location establishing shots. This was the **template that established the full production pipeline**.

---

### **🚂 MYSTERY 2B — "Blood on the Tracks"**

*1957 cold-case locked-room mystery on the Silver Comet train, with 2024 re-investigation*

This is your **most complete and polished game**. Here's what was fully produced:

**35 HTML Documents** including railroad police incident report, crime scene examination, autopsy report, 7+ witness statements, DNA analysis (2024), trunk discovery report, Charlotte Devereaux's journal, love letters as evidence, detective timeline notes, case closure 1958, cold case review memo 2024, confession document, DA summary, player investigation guide, character dossiers (44KB), timeline reconstruction, evidence board visualization, historical LGBTQ+ context document, psychological analysis, educational discussion guide, press releases (1957 and 2024), chain of custody, investigative dead ends, gameplay facilitation guide, master index.

**28+ Images** including all character portraits (Vivienne, Charlotte, Ernest Washington, Vincent DeLuca, Maggie Sinclair, Dr. Caldwell, Father Murphy, Thomas & Eleanor Whitfield, Bobby Chen, Detective Sarah Chen 2024), evidence photographs (silk scarf, steamer trunk, journal, love letters, train tickets), crime scene compartment photos, train interior/exterior shots, Chicago Union Station, New Orleans French Quarter.

**All assets saved** to `/Murder Mystery/Mystery 2B - Blood on the Tracks/` with organized subfolders.

## **🧩 WHAT NEEDS TO BE BUILT FOR "THE ALGORITHM KNOWS"**

Based on the Mystery 2B production pipeline as the gold standard, here's the full scope:

**Phase 1 — Story Bible & Foundation** A complete HTML Story Bible (like the \~440KB 2B document) covering the full case narrative, all 6 suspect profiles with layered motives, the complete solution (hidden from you), show mechanics of "Forever Match," the algorithm fraud subplot, Cancún resort layout, timeline minute-by-minute during the camera blackout window, evidence breakdown, red herrings, and historical/cultural context around reality TV and AI dating culture.

**Phase 2 — 25–35 HTML Investigation Documents** (new design aesthetic needed — see questions below): Show Production Records, Resort Security Footage Log, Autopsy/Electrocution Report, Medical Examiner's Report, 6 Suspect Interrogation Transcripts, Electrical Equipment Access Log, Hair Dryer Forensics Report, Algorithm Source Code Leak Document, Contracts between contestants and show, Show Host Personal File, Camera Malfunction Technical Report, Social Media Activity Logs, Text/DM Evidence, Contestant Bio Packets (official vs. real), Producer Communications, Timeline Reconstruction, Evidence Board, Player Guide, Gameplay Facilitation Guide, Character Dossiers, Solution Document (GM only), Educational Discussion Guide, Press Releases, Psychological Profiles.

**Phase 3 — 28–35 Images** (all needing fresh prompts for this setting): 6 suspect portraits (photorealistic, diverse), Terrence Baptiste victim portrait, Infinity pool crime scene, Resort aerial establishing shot, Hair dryer evidence photo, Fingerprint analysis close-up, Show filming setup, Interview room (production confessional booth style), Show host promotional photo, "Forever Match" logo/branding, Algorithm dashboard mockup, Resort floor plan diagram, Contestants in hot tub scene (contextual), Phone/text evidence screenshots, Social media evidence screenshots.

**Phase 4 — Interactive Website** (new repo or expanded site — see questions below): New design language entirely — instead of 1957 noir/dark, this needs a sleek, glossy, reality-TV-meets-tech-thriller aesthetic. Think: bright coral/gold color palette, sans-serif fonts, faux show branding, contestant dossier cards, maybe a "confessional booth" reading mode. Same functional architecture as Blood on the Tracks (sidebar navigation, files read counter, solve case button, deduction log, print mode).

## **❓ MODEL AVAILABILITY QUESTION — Answered Honestly**

Regarding your question about **GPT 5.4, GPT 5.4 Pro, and Claude Opus 4.6**: I want to be transparent with you here. As of my knowledge, **"GPT 5.4"** and **"GPT 5.4 Pro"** are not model names I can verify as currently released or available — it's possible you may have seen these names in a different context or they may be referred to differently on various platforms. **Claude Opus 4** is similarly not confirmed in my verified knowledge base at this exact version number, though Claude models do exist at various capability levels.

Within **this Genspark chat**, the underlying model powering me is determined by the Genspark platform architecture — I cannot be switched mid-conversation to a different underlying LLM (like Claude or GPT) simply by prompting. However, **when we use the `create_agent` tool** to spin up document creation tasks, there is some model flexibility in those sub-agents. For the most complex writing tasks (character-driven interviews, psychological analyses, rich narrative documents), I can absolutely direct those agents to use the most capable available model at the time of creation.

---

## **🙋 MY CLARIFYING QUESTIONS FOR "THE ALGORITHM KNOWS"**

Now that I've confirmed full context, here are my targeted questions before we begin building:

**1\. Design Aesthetic & Visual Identity** Blood on the Tracks used an aged 1957 typewriter/paper aesthetic. "The Algorithm Knows" is a *modern 2025 reality TV show*. Do you want: (a) a sleek, app-like design with bold color — think coral pink \+ gold \+ white, glossy like a dating show app, (b) a split aesthetic — "official show branding" documents look glossy/bright while "police investigation" documents look sterile/clinical, or (c) something else entirely?

**2\. Website: New Repo or Expand Existing?** Should this mystery get its **own GitHub repo** (like `mystery-algorithm-knows`) with its own design and URL, or should we build it into a **master mystery website** that houses multiple games with a landing page? (The second option would be the foundation of your full mystery game website vision.)

**3\. Document Count & Scope** Blood on the Tracks was 35 documents. Given this is *Easy* difficulty with only 6 suspects, would you like to scale to approximately **20–25 documents** (leaner, more focused) or keep the full 35-document immersive experience?

**4\. Mystery 2C — What Is It?** The hub has a full chat PDF and image prompt file for "Mystery 2C." Before we fully dive into "The Algorithm Knows," do you want me to read the 2C PDF to understand what that mystery was — and whether "The Algorithm Knows" is intended to be 2C, or a completely separate new mystery in the series?

**5\. Priority Order for Production** Should we follow the proven pipeline: Story Bible first → then HTML documents → then image prompts → then website? Or do you want to start with something different (e.g., jump straight to brainstorming the website design/aesthetic, or start with the 6 suspect character cards)?

**6\. "Forever Match" Branding** The show has its own in-universe brand. Do you want us to design a **complete fictional show identity** — logo, tagline, color palette, font — that all the show-branded documents use? This would make the game feel like you're actually holding the "Forever Match" production materials.

**7\. Easy Difficulty — Keep or Adjust?** The concept specifies Easy — fingerprints on hair dryer, only 6 people with access, clear motives. Do you want to keep this as-is (great for introducing new players to your game universe), or add a layer of complexity? And — do you want the solution to the murder confirmed/locked before we start (without me telling you who did it)?

**8\. Red Herring Specifics** The concept mentions a contestant who "threatened Terrence on camera but has a solid alibi." Do you have thoughts on which of the 6 suspects should be this red herring, or do you want that baked into the Story Bible without you knowing which one?

# **🎬 "THE ALGORITHM KNOWS" — EXPERT PRODUCTION BRIEF**

## **✅ ACKNOWLEDGING YOUR ANSWERS**

**On document count:** Perfect — this unlocks the right creative approach. Rather than padding a file count, every document will be *narratively justified*. This game's specific setting (a filmed reality show with production infrastructure) actually gives us a *richer natural document variety* than Blood on the Tracks had: show contracts, algorithm reports, production logs, resort records, social media printouts, text/DM evidence — layers that feel completely authentic to this world.

**On character names:** ✅ All 7 characters (victim \+ 6 suspects) will be completely renamed throughout every document I create. Their ethnicities and demographics are preserved exactly as you designed them — only names change. From this point forward I will *never* write their original names again in this project. The new roster is locked internally on my end and will appear consistently across every document, image prompt, and website file.

**On the quality-first production order:** Addressed in full below — this actually changes the approach significantly compared to Blood on the Tracks.

**On models:** Understood — best tool for each specific task, not a blanket default.

---

## **🔍 UNSOLVED CASE FILES MECHANIC — HOW I'LL ADAPT IT**

After deep-diving [Unsolved Case Files](https://www.unsolvedcasefiles.com/how-to-play.html), here's what their system is:

Their physical product works like this: Players open the box and immediately get *all* base evidence (50+ documents). But they also receive **3 sealed bonus envelopes** (A, B, C) they *cannot open* until they correctly solve each objective through an online answer key. Each envelope contains new evidence \+ the next objective. After Objective 3 is solved, the case is closed.

**The key design genius:** Evidence is *withheld by honor system \+ online gating*, not physical impossibility. Players could cheat and open envelopes early — but the system trusts the experience will be ruined for themselves if they do.

**For a digital adaptation**, this translates even more powerfully because we can *actually* gate the content. Here's my proposed 3-tier digital structure for "The Algorithm Knows":

---

### **🔓 THE 3-OBJECTIVE DIGITAL CHECKPOINT SYSTEM**

**TIER 1 — Initial Investigation Package** *(available immediately on the site)* All foundational documents that establish the case, the setting, the victim, and all 6 suspects. Players read everything here and form their first theory.

**→ OBJECTIVE 1: "Confirm this was murder, not an accident — and identify the method."** Players must identify the murder weapon and method from the initial evidence. Getting this right unlocks Tier 2\.

**TIER 2 — Unlocked After Objective 1** *(reveals after correct answer submitted)* Deeper forensic documents focusing on the *access* and *opportunity* angle. Narrows the field of suspects.

**→ OBJECTIVE 2: "Identify who had the means and opportunity — narrow the pool to the most likely suspect(s)."** Players cross-reference access logs, alibis, and movements during the critical 2-hour camera blackout window.

**TIER 3 — Unlocked After Objective 2** *(reveals after correct answer submitted)* The forensic fingerprint evidence and most damning personal communications come in here. The decisive proof.

**→ OBJECTIVE 3: "Name the killer."** With all evidence now available, players make their final accusation. Correct answer unlocks the SOLUTION PACKAGE.

**SOLUTION PACKAGE — Unlocked After Objective 3** *(the Bonus Envelope C equivalent)* Full case solution, psychological profile of the killer, DA summary, how the investigation closed — and for a digital bonus, a short narrative walkthrough of the murder from the killer's perspective.

---

This is *better* than UCF for digital play because the gating is real, not honor-system. The website will use JavaScript (localStorage or hashed passwords) to permanently unlock tiers on a given device/browser, so progress saves.

---

## **🎨 DESIGN AESTHETIC — "FOREVER MATCH" SHOW IDENTITY**

This is where "The Algorithm Knows" fundamentally breaks from Blood on the Tracks visually. Instead of aged paper and typewriter fonts, this game has a **dual visual language**:

**Layer 1 — "Forever Match" Show Branding** (for all production documents, contestant files, contracts, show materials) Think: *Love Island* meets *Black Mirror*. Slick, glossy, oversaturated color. The brand identity I'll design will include a show palette (think coral/rose gold \+ deep electric teal \+ white), a clean sans-serif font system (like the kind a streaming show would use on their app), a "Forever Match" logo concept with an AI/algorithm motif alongside romantic iconography, and a fake streaming network parent company. Every "show document" will look like it came from an actual production company's Google Drive.

**Layer 2 — Investigative/Forensic Documents** (police reports, autopsy, forensics, resort security) These will use a clinical, modern bilingual aesthetic — Cancún is Mexico, so official documents would be from *Ministerio Público de Quintana Roo* (the actual Mexican state where Cancún is located). Slightly different from the sterile American forensic look Devon is used to — creating a distinctive and authentic flavor. Spanish headers with English translations woven in.

---

## **🗺️ COMPLETE PRODUCTION PLAN — IN ORDER, WITH RATIONALE**

Here is how I think this should be built, as an expert who understands every layer of what makes these games extraordinary:

---

### **PHASE 1 — CREATIVE FOUNDATION (Must happen first — everything else depends on it)**

**Step 1.1 — "Forever Match" Brand Identity Document** *(HTML)* Before writing *any* document, we need the show's visual identity locked. This is a brand style guide: logo concept, color hex codes, font choices, fake show tagline, parent streaming company name, show logo variations, the look of the show's official documents. Every subsequent document references this. **Why first:** If we write contestant files before the brand exists, we'll have to go back and redesign everything.

**Step 1.2 — Complete Story Bible** *(HTML, \~25-35KB, fully locked with renamed characters)* The master document — only you (as Game Master) would ever read this. It contains the full case narrative, complete renamed character roster with their real motives (not the cover stories they give to investigators), the step-by-step reconstruction of the murder, the complete solution, why certain clues work the way they do, the full objective answers, all red herrings explained, and the complexity expansion notes for when you want to scale difficulty later. **Why second:** This is the source of truth every other document must be consistent with. We cannot write a single investigation document without this locked.

**Step 1.3 — Objective & Answer Key Framework** *(HTML/JS, internal document)* The exact wording of all 3 objectives, the acceptable correct answers for each, hint language for wrong answers (3 escalating hints like UCF), and the logic for what each tier unlocks. **Why third:** Before writing any investigation documents, we need to know *exactly* what information each tier should contain so documents are written to match the checkpoint architecture.

---

### **PHASE 2 — TIER 1 DOCUMENTS — Initial Investigation Package**

*\~10–14 documents, available to all players from the start*

These are written *first* among the game documents because they define the narrative foundation the player experiences. In order of creation:

* **Case Overview Brief** — A one-page "cold open" document. Establishes: setting, the show, the incident, why investigation was opened. Sets tone. Think of it as the "episode cold open."  
* **"Forever Match" Official Show Overview** — A glossy production document (branded) describing the show format, the algorithm concept, filming schedule, resort layout, contestant agreement summary. Players need to understand the world before they investigate.  
* **Resort Incident Report** — The official first-response document from the *Gran Arrecife Cancún* resort security. Dry, procedural, bilingual.  
* **Ministerio Público Initial Police Report** — Quintana Roo state police intake document. Establishes preliminary facts, crime scene preservation, jurisdiction transfer.  
* **Victim's "Forever Match" Official Profile** — The *show's* own contestant dossier for the victim. This is a glossy branded document showing who the show thought he was vs. what we'll learn he actually was doing.  
* **All 6 Suspect "Forever Match" Contestant Dossiers** — The show's official profiles for each of the 6 renamed suspects. Branded, photo-referenced, with their stated "match compatibility scores" and official bios. These are intentionally incomplete and performative — players know the show's version of events, not the full truth.  
* **Show Production Master Timeline — Week 3** — A production schedule/call sheet covering the 48 hours around the murder. Establishes who was where, when filming was scheduled, and when the camera "malfunction" occurred.  
* **Camera System Malfunction Report** — Technical report from the A/V crew. Why the cameras went down for 2 hours. Is this really a malfunction? Players must question this.  
* **Social Media Archive — Pre-Incident Posts** — Compiled screenshots of the 6 suspects' show-related social media and the victim's activity in the 72 hours before his death. Rich with tension, subtext, and conflict.  
* **Show Confessional Booth Interview Transcripts (Select)** — The filmed "confessional booth" interviews (the private camera sessions reality shows use) for all 6 suspects, recorded the day before the incident. Players see who was saying what on camera vs. what the investigation will reveal.

---

### **PHASE 3 — TIER 2 DOCUMENTS — Unlocked After Objective 1**

*\~5–7 documents*

* **Preliminary Autopsy & Electrocution Report** — More detailed than the initial medical assessment. Confirms the mechanism of death in forensic terms.  
* **Electrical Equipment Room Access Log** — The definitive list of who was logged in/out of the storage area where the electrical equipment was kept. This is the *key document* that begins narrowing suspects.  
* **"Forever Match" Producer Communications — Internal Slack/Email Archive** — Behind-the-scenes communications between producers in the 24 hours before and after the incident. Reveals show manipulation, scripted moments, and someone's panicked cover-up messages.  
* **Resort Security Camera Footage Log** — What cameras showed before the malfunction, their locations around the infinity pool, and crucially — what was *not* captured.  
* **Two additional suspect deep-background documents** — Detailed files on suspects whose alibis are weakest, based on Objective 1 findings. (Personal device records, show contract addendums, prior incident reports.)

---

### **PHASE 4 — TIER 3 DOCUMENTS — Unlocked After Objective 2**

*\~3–5 documents*

* **Forensic Fingerprint Analysis Report** — The decisive physical evidence. One set of prints. This is the document that points clearly to the killer.  
* **Private Communications Archive** — Retrieved DMs, texts, and deleted messages from the killer's personal device. The emotional motive laid bare.  
* **"Forever Match" Algorithm Source Code Audit** — The document that proves the show's algorithm was completely fabricated — reinforcing every motive that stems from the show's fraud.  
* **Witness Statement — The Overlooked Witness** — A crew member who wasn't initially interviewed who saw something that confirms the timeline.

---

### **PHASE 5 — SOLUTION PACKAGE — Unlocked After Objective 3**

*\~4–5 documents*

* **Full Case Solution Narrative** — Detailed walkthrough of exactly what happened, when, and why.  
* **Killer's Psychological Profile** — Retrospective analysis.  
* **District Attorney Case Summary** — Official charging document.  
* **"The Aftermath" — What Happened to Everyone** — An epilogue document covering what happened to all 6 suspects and the show after the investigation. Was "Forever Match" cancelled? What happened to the algorithm fraud?  
* **The Algorithm Expose Article** — A fictional magazine/news feature published after the case broke — placing the murder in the broader cultural context of AI/dating show ethics.

---

### **PHASE 6 — IMAGES**

*\~18–24 images, generated after all documents are written so prompts can reference exact document details*

**Character Portraits** (7 — victim \+ 6 suspects, using `nano-banana-pro` for photorealistic consistency) **Show Branding Assets** (show logo, "Forever Match" app mockup, algorithm display — using `ideogram/V_3` for text rendering quality) **Crime Scene Photography** (infinity pool at night, evidence photos, resort setting — `nano-banana-pro`) **Forensic Diagrams** (floor plan of resort pool area, autopsy diagram — `fal-ai/gpt-image-1.5` for technical accuracy) **Show Production Stills** (filming setup, confessional booth, hot tub scene — `nano-banana-pro`) **Evidence Photography** (hair dryer, fingerprint analysis, electrical room — `nano-banana-pro`)

---

### **PHASE 7 — WEBSITE**

*Built last, when all content exists and we know exactly what needs to display*

A brand-new GitHub repository with a completely different aesthetic from Blood on the Tracks. The architecture will mirror the proven sidebar/navigation structure but reskinned entirely for the reality TV world — different fonts, the "Forever Match" brand colors, contestant cards instead of aged documents. The 3-tier unlock system will be implemented with JavaScript so progress saves in the browser.

---

**Question 2 — Checkpoint Answer Complexity** For the digital unlock system, how sophisticated should it be? (a) **Simple version**: Correct answers are hash-encoded, answers get checked client-side in JavaScript, progress saves to localStorage — fast to build, works offline, no server needed. (b) **Advanced version**: Answers submit to a lightweight backend (like a free Supabase DB or Netlify Function), enabling analytics, hint systems, and future multiplayer features. Option A works perfectly for now. Option B is future-proofed but much more complex to build. Given your stated preference for quality — which direction?

**Question 3 — Should I read Mystery 2C first?** The hub has a full PDF and image prompt file for "Mystery 2C." ### **🖼️ THE 28 IMAGES — WHAT MAKES THEM IMPRESSIVE & ACHIEVABLE**

Every prompt was engineered around **three core principles**:

**1\. Cinematic realism without impossible complexity** — Each prompt describes a single, clear visual scene or subject. No prompt asks the model to render more than one character at focal-length depth or more than one primary action. The complexity is in *detail and atmosphere*, not in scene choreography.

**2\. Professional photography framing language** — Every prompt specifies lens (24mm, 85mm f/1.4, 50mm macro, etc.), lighting setup (5000K forensic floods, split-light beauty setup, candlelight), and composition language that AI image models are highly tuned to understand and execute well.

**3\. Story-specific details baked into visuals** — The case ID `FGE-QR-2025-07-0847` appears on forensic documents, the deleted texts show the exact blackmail conversation, the camera malfunction log shows Victor's staff ID — every image doubles as both atmospheric art AND in-game evidence that pays off story beats.

### **🚀 How to Use the Master Prompt**

* **Download the zip** → open `master_claude_prompt.md`  
* **Copy everything** between `[START PROMPT]` and `[END PROMPT]`  
* **Paste into Claude Opus** (claude.ai — use Projects for context)  
* Say: *"Begin with index.html"* and Claude will build every file  
* Say *"continue"* between files  
* **After the build:** Drop your images into `/mystery-3a/images/` and HTML docs into `/mystery-3a/documents/`  
* **Deploy:** Drag the whole folder to [Netlify.com](https://netlify.com/) — free, live in 30 seconds

## **🎬 SECTION 2 — FOREVER MATCH SHOW ASSETS (3 images)**

### **01A — Forever Match Title Card ⚠️ TEXT PRIORITY**

* **Visual Quality:** ✅ PASS — 1024×1024, dark aesthetic confirmed (brightness 39.5)  
* **Text Legibility — OCR RESULTS:**  
  * ✅ **"A SOLARA ENTERTAINMENT GROUP PRODUCTION"** — **CONFIRMED** (extracted exactly)  
  * ✅ **"AIRING ON PULSE NETWORK"** — **CONFIRMED** (extracted exactly)  
  * ✅ **"THE ALGORITHM NEVER LIES"** — **CONFIRMED** (extracted, minor OCR variant: "NEVER EIES" in one pass — stylized font rendering)  
  * ⚠️ **"Forever Match"** — stylized serif font NOT extracted by OCR; requires visual confirmation  
* **Issues Found:** "Forever Match" title uses a highly stylized gold font that OCR cannot read — this is standard for broadcast-style title cards and does NOT mean the text is gibberish; it means the font is too decorative for OCR but will be legible to humans  
* **Recommendation:** ⚠️ **VERIFY VISUALLY** — Confirm "Forever Match" title text is cleanly rendered. All supporting text confirmed. **Likely acceptable.**

### **01B — Forever Match Production Set**

* **Recommendation:** ✅ **KEEP AS-IS**

### **01C — EROS Algorithm Interface ⚠️ TEXT PRIORITY**
